    <overall_goal>
        Implement the BatchUpdateByCondition feature, providing a fluent API for high-performance batch updates using dynamic, potentially heterogeneous conditions.
    </overall_goal>

    <key_knowledge>
        - Project Structure: Monorepo with `core` (engine) and `spring` (integration) modules.
        - TDD Workflow: Writing unit tests before implementation is mandatory.
        - SPI Registration: New Execution classes must be registered in `META-INF/services/...Execution`.
        - MybatisHelper: Updated to support `batchUpdates(List&lt;BatchItem&gt; items, int batchSize)` where each item contains a unique SQL string and its context, allowing heterogeneous WHERE clauses in a single batch session.
        - Naming Convention: Fixed an inconsistency where `BaseService` expected `onlyUpdateNonNull` but `BaseDao` provided `updateOnlyNonNull`. The standard is now `onlyUpdateNonNull`.
        - Checkpoints: Phase 1 (Foundations) SHA `cc0df89`; Phase 2 (Execution Engine) SHA `a4dcbc4`.
    </key_knowledge>

## MODEL âœ¨

I'll perform comprehensive integration testing. I've already added several unit tests:
1. `MybatisHelperBatchUpdatesTest`: Verifies the low-level `MybatisHelper.batchUpdates` works with heterogeneous SQL.
2. `BatchUpdateByConditionExecutionTest`: Verifies the execution engine correctly translates `BatchUpdateByConditionCommand` to SQL/Contexts.
3. `BatchUpdateByConditionChainTest`: Verifies the fluent API correctly builds and executes the command.

Now I'll add a more complex integration test that verifies interceptors and events as well.

I'll create `core/src/test/java/io/github/myacelw/mybatis/dynamic/core/service/BatchUpdateByConditionIntegrationTest.java`.

```java
package io.github.myacelw.mybatis.dynamic.core.service;

import io.github.myacelw.mybatis.dynamic.core.event.data.BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent;
import io.github.myacelw.mybatis.dynamic.core.metadata.vo.FieldValue;
import io.github.myacelw.mybatis.dynamic.core.service.execution.BaseExecutionTest;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicInteger;

import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertEquals;
import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertTrue;

class BatchUpdateByConditionIntegrationTest extends BaseExecutionTest {

    @Test
    void testIntegrationWithInterceptorsAndEvents() {
        DataManager<String> dataManager = getDataManager("User");
        
        AtomicInteger beforeCount = new AtomicInteger(0);
        AtomicInteger afterCount = new AtomicInteger(0);
        AtomicInteger eventCount = new AtomicInteger(0);

        // Add Interceptor
        dataManager.getModelContext().getInterceptors().add(new DataChangeInterceptor() {
            @Override
            public void beforeBatchUpdateByCondition(DataManager<Object> dm, List<?> updates) {
                beforeCount.incrementAndGet();
                assertEquals(2, updates.size());
            }

            @Override
            public void afterBatchUpdateByCondition(DataManager<Object> dm, List<?> updates) {
                afterCount.incrementAndGet();
                assertEquals(2, updates.size());
            }
        });

        // Add Event Listener
        dataManager.getModelContext().getEventListeners().add(event -> {
            if (event instanceof BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent) {
                eventCount.incrementAndGet();
                BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent e = (BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent) event;
                assertEquals(2, e.getUpdatePairs().size());
            }
        });

        Map<String, Object> data1 = new HashMap<>();
        data1.put("name", "Integrate 1");
        
        Map<String, Object> data2 = new HashMap<>();
        data2.put("name", "Integrate 2");

        dataManager.batchUpdateByConditionChain()
                .add(c -> c.eq("id", "u1"), data1)
                .add(c -> c.eq("id", "u2"), data2)
                .exec();

        // Verify counts
        assertEquals(1, beforeCount.get());
        assertEquals(1, afterCount.get());
        assertEquals(1, eventCount.get());

        // Verify Data
        assertEquals("Integrate 1", dataManager.getById("u1").get("name"));
        assertEquals("Integrate 2", dataManager.getById("u2").get("name"));
    }
}
```

Wait, `dataManager.getModelContext().getInterceptors()` might not be directly modifiable if it's a list. I'll check `ModelContext.java`.

## MODEL âœ¨

Yes, `interceptors` is a mutable `ArrayList`.

I'll write the integration test.

**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "core/src/test/java/io/github/myacelw/mybatis/dynamic/core/service/BatchUpdateByConditionIntegrationTest.java",
    "content": "package io.github.myacelw.mybatis.dynamic.core.service;\n\nimport io.github.myacelw.mybatis.dynamic.core.event.data.BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent;\nimport io.github.myacelw.mybatis.dynamic.core.service.execution.BaseExecutionTest;\nimport org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;\n\nimport java.util.HashMap;\nimport java.util.List;\nimport java.util.Map;\nimport java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicInteger;\n\nimport static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertEquals;\n\nclass BatchUpdateByConditionIntegrationTest extends BaseExecutionTest {\n\n    @Test\n    void testIntegrationWithInterceptorsAndEvents() {\n        DataManager<String> dataManager = getDataManager(\"User\");\n\n        AtomicInteger beforeCount = new AtomicInteger(0);\n        AtomicInteger afterCount = new AtomicInteger(0);\n        AtomicInteger eventCount = new AtomicInteger(0);\n\n        // Add Interceptor\n        dataManager.getModelContext().getInterceptor().getInterceptors().add(new DataChangeInterceptor() {\n            @Override\n            public void beforeBatchUpdateByCondition(DataManager<Object> dm, List<?> updates) {\n                beforeCount.incrementAndGet();\n                assertEquals(2, updates.size());\n            }\n\n            @Override\n            public void afterBatchUpdateByCondition(DataManager<Object> dm, List<?> updates) {\n                afterCount.incrementAndGet();\n                assertEquals(2, updates.size());\n            }\n        });\n\n        // Add Event Listener\n        dataManager.getModelContext().getEventListeners().add(event -> {\n            if (event instanceof BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent) {\n                eventCount.incrementAndGet();\n                BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent e = (BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent) event;\n                assertEquals(2, e.getUpdatePairs().size());\n            }\n        });\n\n        Map<String, Object> data1 = new HashMap<>();\n        data1.put(\"name\", \"Integrate 1\");\n\n        Map<String, Object> data2 = new HashMap<>();\n        data2.put(\"name\", \"Integrate 2\");\n\n        dataManager.batchUpdateByConditionChain()\n                .add(c -> c.eq(\"id\", \"u1\"), data1)\n                .add(c -> c.eq(\"id\", \"u2\"), data2)\n                .exec();\n\n        // Verify counts\n        assertEquals(1, beforeCount.get());\n        assertEquals(1, afterCount.get());\n        assertEquals(1, eventCount.get());\n\n        // Verify Data\n        assertEquals(\"Integrate 1\", dataManager.getById(\"u1\").get(\"name\"));\n        assertEquals(\"Integrate 2\", dataManager.getById(\"u2\").get(\"name\"));\n    }\n}\n"
  }
}

## MODEL âœ¨

The line 40 is indeed the interceptor addition.

Wait, I see:
```java
this.interceptor = new DataChangeInterceptorGroup(interceptors == null ? Collections.emptyList() : interceptors);
```
in `ModelContext`.

If `interceptors` was null, it uses `Collections.emptyList()`.
Then `getInterceptors()` returns `Collections.emptyList()`.
And `add(...)` on it throws `UnsupportedOperationException`.

Wait, the error reported was `NullPointerException`.

Maybe `dataManager.getModelContext()` is returning null?
In `ModelServiceImpl.java`:
```java
    @Override
    public <ID> DataManager<ID> getDataManager(String modelName, SqlSession sqlSession) {
        Model model = getModel(modelName);
        if (model == null) {
            return null;
        }
        ModelContext modelContext = new ModelContext(model, dialect, mybatisHelper, this, fillers, permission, eventListeners, interceptors, sqlSession);
        return new DataManagerImpl<>(modelContext);
    }
```
If `model` is null, it returns null.

But if `dataManager` was null, line 40 would throw NPE at `dataManager.getModelContext()`.

Wait, I'll check `DataChangeInterceptorGroup` implementation again.

```java
public class DataChangeInterceptorGroup implements DataChangeInterceptor {

    @Getter
    private final List<DataChangeInterceptor> interceptors;

    public DataChangeInterceptorGroup(List<DataChangeInterceptor> interceptors) {
        this.interceptors = interceptors == null ? Collections.emptyList() : new ArrayList<>(interceptors);
    }
```

Wait! If `interceptors` is null, it uses `Collections.emptyList()`.
BUT, if I use `new ArrayList<>(Collections.emptyList())`, it's a mutable list.
Actually, the code is:
`this.interceptors = interceptors == null ? Collections.emptyList() : new ArrayList<>(interceptors);`

Ah! If `interceptors` is NULL, it uses `Collections.emptyList()` DIRECTLY!
It does NOT wrap it in `new ArrayList<>()` in the null case.

```java
this.interceptors = interceptors == null ? Collections.emptyList() : new ArrayList<>(interceptors);
```

So if `interceptors` is null, `this.interceptors` IS `Collections.emptyList()`.
Then `getInterceptors().add(...)` fails.

Wait, why `NullPointerException` instead of `UnsupportedOperationException`?
Lombok's `@Getter`? No.

Maybe `ModelContext`'s `getInterceptor()` returns null? No, it's final.

I'll check `ModelContext.java` again very carefully.

```java
    @Getter
    private final DataChangeInterceptorGroup interceptor;
```

Wait, `interceptor` (singular) vs `interceptors` (plural).

In `ModelContext` constructor:
```java
this.interceptor = new DataChangeInterceptorGroup(interceptors == null ? Collections.emptyList() : interceptors);
```

I'll try to use a more robust way to add the interceptor, or just fix `DataChangeInterceptorGroup` to always use a mutable list.

But wait, why `NullPointerException`?

I'll debug by adding some print statements or splitting the line.

Actually, I'll check `BaseExecutionTest.java` again.
It calls `modelService = new ModelServiceBuilder(sqlSessionFactory).fillers(fillers).tablePrefix("d_").build();`.
It doesn't set interceptors, so they are likely null in `ModelContext`.

I'll fix `DataChangeInterceptorGroup.java` to always use a mutable list.

```java
    public DataChangeInterceptorGroup(List<DataChangeInterceptor> interceptors) {
        this.interceptors = interceptors == null ? new ArrayList<>() : new ArrayList<>(interceptors);
    }
```

## MODEL âœ¨

I'll also check `ModelContext.java` for `eventListeners`.

```java
    @Getter
    private final List<EventListener> eventListeners;
...
    public ModelContext(..., List<EventListener> eventListeners, ...) {
...
        this.eventListeners = eventListeners;
```

If `eventListeners` is null, `getEventListeners().add(...)` will definitely throw `NullPointerException`.

In `ModelServiceBuilder.java`:
```java
    public ModelService build() {
...
        return new ModelServiceImpl(..., eventListeners, ...);
    }
```
If not set, `eventListeners` is null.

I should fix `ModelContext` to handle null `eventListeners` by making it an empty mutable list as well.

Actually, I'll fix `BatchUpdateByConditionIntegrationTest.java` to handle null lists or I'll fix the core classes. Fixing core classes is better for extensibility.

é«˜çº§åŠŸèƒ½\n\n##### æ”¯æŒè¡Œæƒé™å’Œåˆ—æƒé™ç®¡ç†ï¼Œå‚è§ `Permission` ç±»ï¼›\n\n1. è¡Œæƒé™ï¼šå®é™…ä¸Šæ˜¯æŸ¥è¯¢æ¡ä»¶ï¼Œå¯¹è¯¥æ¨¡å‹æŸ¥è¯¢æ˜¯éƒ½ä¼šé™„åŠ ä¸Šè¡Œæƒé™è¿‡æ»¤æ¡ä»¶ï¼Œæ”¯æŒä¸ºç©ºï¼›\n2. ç°åœ¨æ”¯æŒæ›´åŠ è‡ªç„¶å’Œå¼ºå¤§çš„é“¾å¼è°ƒç”¨ APIï¼Œå¯ä»¥æ–¹ä¾¿åœ°æ„é€ å¤æ‚çš„ `AND`ã€`OR`ã€`NOT` ç»„åˆæ¡ä»¶ï¼Œå¹¶è‡ªåŠ¨å¤„ç†é€»è¾‘ä¼˜å…ˆçº§ï¼ˆAND ä¼˜å…ˆçº§é«˜äº ORï¼‰ã€‚\n\nç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š\n*   **SQL:** `a = 1 AND (b > 2 OR c < 3) AND d = 4`\n*   **ä»£ç :**\n    ```java\n    cb.eq(\"a\", 1)\n      .and(b -> b.gt(\"b\", 2).or(b2 -> b2.lt(\"c\", 3)))\n      .eq(\"d\", 4)\n    ```\n    æˆ–è€…ä½¿ç”¨æ›´æ˜¾å¼çš„é“¾å¼é£æ ¼ï¼š\n    ```java\n    cb.eq(\"a\", 1)\n      .and().bracket(b -> b.gt(\"b\", 2).or().lt(\"c\", 3))\n      .and().eq(\"d\", 4)\n    ```\n\n**ä¸»è¦ç‰¹æ€§ï¼š**\n*   **é€»è¾‘è¿æ¥è¯:** æä¾› `and()`ã€`or()`ã€`not()` æ–¹æ³•è¿›è¡Œé€»è¾‘åˆ‡æ¢ã€‚\n*   **æ‹¬å·æ”¯æŒ:** `bracket(Consumer<ConditionBuilder>)` ç”¨äºåˆ›å»ºæ˜¾å¼çš„æ‹¬å·åˆ†ç»„ã€‚\n*   **ä¼˜å…ˆçº§å¤„ç†:** è‡ªåŠ¨å¤„ç† `A AND B OR C` (è§†ä¸º `(A AND B) OR C`) å’Œ `A OR B AND C` (è§†ä¸º `A OR (B AND C)`)ã€‚\n*   **ä»£ç å¤ç”¨:** æ‰€æœ‰çš„è¿æ¥è¯è¿”å›çš„ Connector éƒ½å…·å¤‡å®Œæ•´çš„æ¡ä»¶æ„é€ èƒ½åŠ›ï¼ˆeq, gt, in, etc.ï¼‰ï¼Œå‡å°‘ä»£ç é‡å¤ã€‚\n\n1. é€šè¿‡è®¾ç½®`joins`å±æ€§ï¼ŒæŸ¥è¯¢æ¥å£æ”¯æŒæ‰©å±•æŸ¥è¯¢ä¸»è¡¨çš„åŒæ—¶æŸ¥è¯¢å‡ºå­—æ®µä¸º å…³è”ç±»å‹`ToOne`ã€`ToMany`çš„å…·ä½“å…³è”è¡¨çš„æ•°æ®ã€‚\n2. JoinæŸ¥è¯¢è®¾ç½®ï¼Œè¯´æ˜ï¼š\n   ä¸‹é¢ç»™ä¸€ä¸ªå…¸å‹æ¨¡å‹åœºæ™¯å¹¶ç»™å‡ºå‡ ä¸ªé…ç½®çš„ä¾‹å­ï¼š\n   æ¨¡å‹é…ç½®ï¼š\n\n* æ¨¡å‹ Userï¼Œå­—æ®µ departments: ToMany(Department) ;\n* æ¨¡å‹ Department ï¼Œå­—æ®µ ### æ‰¹é‡æ ¹æ®æ¡ä»¶æ›´æ–° (Batch Update By Condition)

`DataManager` (Core) å’Œ `BaseDao`/`BaseService` (Spring) æä¾›äº† `batchUpdateByConditionChain()` æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæ”¯æŒåœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªæ‰¹å¤„ç†ä¼šè¯ä¸­æ‰§è¡Œå¤šä¸ªå¸¦æœ‰ä¸åŒæ›´æ–°æ•°æ®å’Œä¸åŒ WHERE æ¡ä»¶çš„æ›´æ–°è¯­å¥ã€‚

        .add(c -> c.eq(User::getId, "u1"), data1)

```

## MODEL âœ¨

I have completed the implementation of the `BatchUpdateByCondition` feature.

**Summary of Changes:**
1.  **Core Engine Extensions:**
    *   Enhanced `MybatisHelper` to support batch updates with heterogeneous SQL statements in a single session.
    *   Implemented `BatchUpdateByConditionExecution` to translate high-level commands into low-level batch operations.
    *   Registered the new execution engine via SPI.
    *   Added `BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent` for event-driven workflows.
    *   Added `beforeBatchUpdateByCondition` and `afterBatchUpdateByCondition` hooks to `DataChangeInterceptor`.
2.  **Fluent API:**
    *   Implemented `BatchUpdateByConditionChain` for a builder-style update experience.
    *   Exposed the fluent API in `DataManager` (Core), `BaseDao`, and `BaseService` (Spring).
3.  **Stability Improvements:**
    *   Fixed a naming inconsistency (`onlyUpdateNonNull` vs `updateOnlyNonNull`) between Core and Spring modules.
    *   Ensured `ModelContext` and `DataChangeInterceptorGroup` always use mutable lists for listeners and interceptors, preventing NPEs/UOE during runtime extension.
4.  **Verification:**
    *   Added comprehensive unit and integration tests covering SQL generation, execution, events, and interceptors.
    *   Verified the feature in both standalone (Core) and Spring Boot environments.
    *   Ensured project-wide build success.
5.  **Documentation:**
    *   Updated `README.md` with usage examples for the new API.

The track `batch_update_by_condition_20260115` is now complete.

<state_snapshot>
    <overall_goal>
        Implement the BatchUpdateByCondition feature, providing a fluent API for high-performance batch updates using dynamic, potentially heterogeneous conditions.
    </overall_goal>

    <key_knowledge>
        - Project Structure: Monorepo with `core` (engine) and `spring` (integration) modules.
        - TDD Workflow: Writing unit tests before implementation is mandatory.
        - SPI Registration: New Execution classes must be registered in `META-INF/services/...Execution`.
        - MybatisHelper: Updated to support `batchUpdates(List&lt;BatchItem&gt; items, int batchSize)` where each item contains a unique SQL string and its context, allowing heterogeneous WHERE clauses in a single batch session.
        - Naming Convention: Fixed an inconsistency where `BaseService` expected `onlyUpdateNonNull` but `BaseDao` provided `updateOnlyNonNull`. The standard is now `onlyUpdateNonNull`.
        - Resilience: Updated `ModelContext` and `DataChangeInterceptorGroup` to ensure `eventListeners` and `interceptors` lists are always mutable and non-null.
        - Checkpoints: Phase 1 (cc0df89), Phase 2 (a4dcbc4), Phase 3 (2130823), Phase 4 (2a8650e).
    </key_knowledge>

    <file_system_state>
        - conductor/tracks/batch_update_by_condition_20260115/plan.md: [MODIFIED] All phases marked as complete with checkpoint SHAs.
        - README.md: [MODIFIED] Added documentation for the new Batch Update API.
        - core/src/main/java/io/github/myacelw/mybatis/dynamic/core/service/command/BatchUpdateByConditionCommand.java: [CREATED] Holds `List&lt;UpdatePair&gt;`.
        - core/src/main/java/io/github/myacelw/mybatis/dynamic/core/event/data/BatchUpdateByConditionDataEvent.java: [CREATED] Event for the new batch operation.
        - core/src/main/java/io/github/myacelw/mybatis/dynamic/core/database/impl/MybatisHelperImpl.java: [MODIFIED] Implemented multi-SQL batching.
        - core/src/main/java/io/github/myacelw/mybatis/dynamic/core/service/execution/BatchUpdateByConditionExecution.java: [CREATED] Core execution logic.
        - core/src/main/java/io/github/myacelw/mybatis/dynamic/core/service/chain/BatchUpdateByConditionChain.java: [CREATED] Fluent API implementation.
        - spring/src/main/java/io/github/myacelw/mybatis/dynamic/spring/dao/BaseDao.java: [MODIFIED] Added fluent API and fixed naming inconsistency.
        - core/src/test/java/io/github/myacelw/mybatis/dynamic/core/service/BatchUpdateByConditionIntegrationTest.java: [CREATED] Comprehensive integration test.
    </file_system_state>

    <recent_actions>
        - Fixed `NullPointerException` in integration tests by ensuring `eventListeners` and `interceptors` lists are initialized as mutable `ArrayList`s in `ModelContext` and `DataChangeInterceptorGroup`.

        - Executed global project build (`mvn clean install`) which passed.
